name:Mâ€sâ€xâ€iâ€aâ€oâ€qâ€iâ€aâ€o

posted:Posted April 13, 2024
msg:I booked a twin room with full sea view. I wanted to change the itinerary and cancel it about an hour after booking, but the hotel refused to cancel it. I called and they first blamed Ctrip, saying that Ctrip did not cancel it for them. I called Ctrip customer service, and Ctrip customer service contacted me immediately. The merchant told Ctrip that they would charge a 35% penalty. Oh, I could bargain to 20%... I thought, forget it, I'll go...

When I arrived at the hotel, in order to compensate for my unhappiness, when I said I would leave early tomorrow morning, they told me that I could check out at 2 pm, but it was impossible to upgrade the room because it was full. I don't understand why they didn't let me cancel it when it was full?

The underground parking lot is not directly connected to the hotel. You have to change the elevator after nine twists and turns. Then you have to go to the front desk to scan the code and register every time you go out. It's better to park on the ground.

When I entered the room, the small refrigerator was locked. It was the first time I encountered it. There was no signal when I turned on the TV. The TV in such a large room seemed to be 50 or 55, which was very small. After reporting the TV failure, we went out, and the TV didn't even reset when we came back.
The room had four bottles of 350ml water. To compensate me, I was told that if I needed extra mineral water, I could ask the waiter. The waiter came to adjust the air conditioner and TV for us. We asked the waiter to get some water. She said that the door was not closed and she would bring it immediately. Then we waited for more than half an hour and got two bottles. I really thank her!
When I went to the front desk to scan the code to register the license plate, I was told that the room scale was out of power. The front desk said that it would be arranged immediately. When I returned to the hotel at night, it was still the same. It was out of power and had not been moved...
Alas, I have never seen such a bad five-star hotel...

name:Sâ€hâ€uâ€zâ€hâ€uâ€dâ€eâ€nâ€iâ€u
info:Castle Deluxe Room - Lake-View (2 beds)
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:15 Reviews
rating:2.2
posted:Posted February 23, 2024
msg:The entire stay was the most unpleasant experience during my Spring Festival holiday, which made me lose the mood to travel. I checked out early in the morning and returned directly. First, I searched for hotels in Shanwei on Ctrip in advance, because there were fewer hotels with twin beds during the Spring Festival, and my child was a little uncomfortable during the trip. I lived by the sea, so I didnâ€™t choose a sea view room on the beach. I chose a 5-star hotel in the city, hoping to get good service so that my child could recover well. Generally, travel guides recommend Shantou more. The reason why I chose Shanwei was that I was curious to see what the differences were between the two cities. However, I really regretted it! 
1: The price on the page that popped up when I used Gaode Navigation to go to the hotel was 100 yuan cheaper than the one booked by Ctrip. It was relatively smooth to contact Ctrip customer service to refund the price difference, but as a long-time customer, I felt that I was ripped off. 
2: We checked into the hotel at 5:00, and the front desk told us that the room had not been cleaned up yet. This was out of the ordinary. Normally, we check out at 12:00, but it had been more than 5 hours, and the room had not been cleaned up yet. The front desk receptionist asked us to wait on the sofa in the lobby, and did not give us a glass of water or apologize. Instead, a hotel customer service representative came and kept recommending the half-price buffet. Since we wanted to make up for it, we bought one. After waiting for half an hour, they hurriedly arranged a room. We booked a lake view room, and we were satisfied with the room facilities and scenery. So when we checked in, we found that bathrobes, bath towels, mineral water, and face towels were all missing, so we asked the room lady to get them ourselves (we had just finished cleaning and were still cleaning next door). We brought our children to check in, and we didn't ask for more, just the standard room for 2 people. Why do you say this? Because there was a reversal later. 3: After checking in, we went out for dinner (because the hotel buffet and restaurant had no extra seats and extra ingredients, and the buffet restaurant was not enough, which was a bit incomprehensible, but we understood that it was the Spring Festival, and there were many delicious foods in Shanwei, so we went out to eat). We returned to the hotel at around 9 o'clock and found that the welcome fruit promised when booking had not been given, so we called the front desk. At this time, we found that the room phone was not connected and the TV was also broken. We called the front desk with our mobile phone. After the first call was connected, no one came for half an hour. During this time, we found that there was a pair of slippers of the original guest under the bed that had not been cleared away. We were worried that the room hygiene was not done well, so we called 4 more times in succession. The 4th call was connected, and we insisted on being transferred to the complaint depar**ent, but they said there was none. We asked the account manager to handle it. After the front desk agreed, they didn't come after about 10 minutes, so we called again and they said the front desk manager was on the way. After waiting for another 2 or 3 minutes, a so-called front desk manager came to the door. Regarding the check-in issues, the welcome fruit plate, the room hygiene, and the facilities, he repeatedly explained that there was too much guests to serve, and he was very tired, etc., but there was no sincere apology or compensation measures (he proposed to send a breakfast to the children, but we said we had already bought it, so we didn't say it was free). Because it was close to 10 o'clock, we asked for the room sheets and quilt covers to be changed again, and proposed to deal with it the next day. The front desk manager said that he was not available the next day (as a result, when we checked out the next day, he was leisurely at the front desk and had nothing to deal with. When we checked out, he pretended not to know him). What was particularly funny was that there were 4 bottles of water in our room at that time, and the front desk manager insisted that we asked for 4 bottles. We explained that we asked the cleaning staff for 2 bottles when we checked in, and we didn't know if the last two bottles were put in later. A five-star hotel has so many service problems. It is ridiculous that it does not apologize or solve them, but comes to entangle us whether we asked for 4 bottles of water.
3. To be fair, the hotel's hardware facilities and environment are good, and the hotel is garden-style, but the service quality and level are not as good as the Hanting and All Seasons where we stayed.
4. The breakfast is not up to the standard of a five-star hotel. If it is not free, it is better to go out for morning tea.
5. After staying in this hotel, I have no mood to play again. The impression of Shanwei is so-so.
6. Later, I saw a few people talking about this hotel on Xiaohongshu. They also said that they have stayed for 3 consecutive years, and the service is getting worse every year. I will never stay there again.
